Local News: Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, Shanghai, etc.

Seawall Repairs Completed, No Worries for Autumn Floods

Repair of Seawall Projects in Progress

Supervisory Committee Sets Out for Inspection

The seawalls of Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, Nanhui, Shanghai and other places suffered significant damage from several typhoons and tidal surges last autumn. In addition to emergency repairs at the time, funds were raised for repairs. The seawall projects in various places are now being completed in succession, and there should be no danger of autumn floods this year. Details are as follows:

Taicang and Baoshan Seawalls to be Completed Soon

The seawalls of Jiading, Taicang, and Baoshan suffered the most severe damage last autumn. Local governments and people repeatedly appealed to the provincial government, requesting funds for repairs. The provincial government approved a large sum, and since the county authorities started the repairs this spring, the Jiading side was completed last month. Taicang and Baoshan are also expected to be fully completed by the end of this month. Once the project is completed, a report will be submitted to the provincial authorities, requesting them to send personnel for inspection and acceptance.

Pudong and Puxi to Start Construction Soon

The seawalls of Gaoqiao in Pudong and Wusong in Puxi, which were damaged by both the January 28th Incident and the autumn typhoons, urgently need repair. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works believes that these two seawalls are crucial to the security of the city, so it has prepared a detailed plan and submitted it to the municipal government for approval. It has advertised for contractors to bid on the project, and bidding will open next week. Construction will begin immediately and must be completed before the autumn floods to avoid danger.

Provincial Authorities Inspect and Accept Nanhui Seawall Project

The seventy-plus li of seawalls along the coast in eastern Nanhui County were almost completely destroyed during the autumn floods last year. County Magistrate Yuan Xiluo submitted a request to the provincial government for a large sum of money, and he worked with local gentry to carry out repairs. The entire project was completed by the end of last month and has been submitted to the provincial authorities for filing. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction sent personnel to the county the other day for inspection and acceptance. The entire project was repaired very well, and there should be no danger during the autumn floods this year.

Supervisory Committee Sets Out for Inspection

In order to emphasize the importance of repairing seawalls, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has specially hired seven gentry from Jiading, Taicang, and Baoshan, including Zhang Gongquan, Zhu Kaichou, Zhao Housheng, Jin Houcheng, Hong Shengping, Shen Siqi, and Min Ruizhi, as members of the Jiangnan Seawall Supervisory Committee. In addition to visiting various places for inspection at any time, now that the seawall projects in various places are about to be completed in succession and the autumn floods are approaching, all the committee members plan to go to Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan, and other places for a week-long inspection of the repair situation within days. It is predicted that the cities and regions near this city will be safe from danger for this year's autumn floods.

Gaoqiao Farmers Suffer from Drought

Appeal for Removal of Old Huangpu Dyke

Agricultural Association Reports on the Investigation

Bureau Approves Removal; Agricultural Association Responsible

This summer, due to the severe drought, the Gaoqiao district farmers, with their fields cracked and the autumn harvest hopeless, recently started a spontaneous trend of demolishing the high dike built by the Junpu Bureau in the Old Huangpu, hoping that the tide would flow in to irrigate the farmland. A reporter from the Great White Society, after learning of this, went to various places to investigate the details, which are described below:

Reasons for Demolishing the Dyke

According to the person in charge of the Municipal Agricultural Association, since the beginning of this year's drought, villagers in various districts have been asking the municipal authorities and the Municipal Agricultural Association for quick relief. The Drought Prevention Association was immediately organized, and the Social Affairs and Public Works Bureaus worked together to implement drought relief measures. A large number of water pumps were purchased and distributed to various villages, and the Junpu Bureau and fire trucks were asked to help pump water. However, the cost was high and the effect was minimal, so it was soon stopped. The coastal areas could have been irrigated by the tide during high tide, but since the Junpu Bureau started building the dike, the tide has been blocked. Therefore, the farmers in the Gaoqiao district, in order to save themselves, resorted to demolishing the dike. After learning of this, the Municipal Party Department sent Zhang Huijun, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Tian Heqing, and the Municipal Agricultural Association sent Yu Zhenhui to investigate the truth in order to verify and handle the matter.

Municipal Agricultural Association Report

The Municipal Agricultural Association reported to the Social Affairs Bureau, stating that the Gaoqiao district farmers requested to demolish the dam. In order to be informed of the matter, the Association had previously reported that the Junpu Bureau was building a dam in the Old Huangpu, blocking the tide and causing insufficient water for irrigation, resulting in the drying up of branch rivers. The Association immediately reported the situation for relief, and the Bureau sent personnel to contact the Junpu Bureau, which agreed to pump water for six hours every night from the 2nd. However, the farmers still complained that the water was insufficient. On the afternoon of the 3rd, they gathered at the home of Lu Dong, a preparation member of the district agricultural association, to protest. Upon hearing the news, the Association sent personnel to the Bureau and the Municipal Government on the morning of the 4th to report and request immediate measures to pump water day and night. The Bureau and the Municipal Government then sent personnel to contact the Junpu Bureau, which agreed to pump water continuously for sixty hours starting on the evening of the 4th. On the afternoon of the same day (the 4th), Director Tian Heqing of the Bureau, together with the Association, went to investigate. When they arrived near Lingjiazhai, the farmers were gathering with gongs. They, along with Director Tian, advised them to be good. The farmers from various villages still came in groups, stating that since the construction of the dam in the Old Huangpu (which had once collapsed on the evening of July 22 and was later rebuilt), the tide has been blocked. They had hoped that the Junpu Bureau would pump water, but they were only pumping for two or three hours a day (and said that due to insufficient pumping, there was occasional muddy water mixed into the river, which easily caused blockage and was of no help). Only the Old Huangpu had water, while all other branch rivers had dried up. They also heard rumors that the Junpu Bureau was planning to fill the Old Huangpu and sell it, so they went in the morning to demolish the dam, etc. At that time, the farmers gathered in greater numbers, and together they went to the Third District and Fourth Precinct Office of Gaoqiao Town, pointing out the drying up of rivers and the withering of fields along the way. Some of them were crying in pain and shedding tears, and their situation was particularly pitiful. Director Zhan and Director Tian advised them to be kind and discussed the farmers' demands: (1) Please demolish the dam built in the Old Huangpu within three days to allow the tide to pass through; (2) Dredge the rivers; (3) Provide relief; (4) Exempt taxes. At that time, the crowd was agitated, and they had no choice but to consult with Director Tian and Director Zhan. They agreed to report the demands to the Municipal Government for approval before dispersing, threatening to gather again to appeal if the dam was not demolished within three days. They returned to Shanghai with Director Tian and reported the situation in detail. Yesterday (the 5th), they went with Director Tian to advise and supervise the installation of the East Sea water pump. The situation has been reported in detail. Please approve.

Instructions from the Social Affairs Bureau

Received. The dam built by the Junpu Bureau in the Huangpu River is no longer needed and is being urged for removal. Since this is a common request, it should be approved for removal. However, the Association should be responsible for any water conservancy and other problems that may arise after the dam's removal. In addition to reporting the matter and the other requests, a report will be submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. This is the approval.

Hurricane Gone

Yesterday was Sunny and Hot as Usual

Navigation of Jianghai Vessels Returns to Normal

After the Pacific typhoon passed Shanghai the other day, it is now heading north. An inquiry was made to the local observatory yesterday, which stated that the report at 6:00 AM (yesterday) indicated that the storm had reached 33 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude, heading north-northeast and then due north. However, the observatory continued to report at 2:00 PM that the storm had reached 35 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude, heading north or north-northeast. Therefore, it is predicted that the storm was in the Yellow Sea (i.e., Haizhou) between Mokpo, Korea, at 2:00 PM. If it does not change direction and continues to blow north, it will make landfall in Andong, at the border between Korea and Liaoning. As for the rumor that there were still six degrees of wind force lingering on Dajishan outside Songkou yesterday morning, it is completely untrue. At the same time, the observatory stated that a new typhoon has occurred in the Pacific, but it is still far from land and no detailed reports have been received. As for yesterday's temperature, due to the passage of the typhoon the other day, it dropped sharply to 81.4 degrees, but yesterday it was sunny and hot as usual, with a high of 94.8 degrees and a low of 75.9 degrees, seemingly returning to the state it was three days ago. The vessels that were blocked have now entered the port one after another and have resumed their schedules. Details are as follows:

Reasons for Shuntian's Entry and Retreat

The Taikoo Company's Shuntian Wheel, after changing its route to the Yangtze River, operates between Hankou and Shanghai and to various ports in the north and south. On the 8th, the ship arrived in Shanghai at 2:00 PM. The ship had entered the port and sailed to Yangshupu when it suddenly turned back to the outside of Wusongkou. The company did not know the reason at the time and sent a telegram to inquire. It was not until yesterday morning that Shuntian entered the port again. According to the crew, when the ship was entering the port, it was difficult to berth at the dock due to the strong winds and turbulent waters of the Pudong River. Therefore, it turned back to Wusongkou and anchored for one night, and opened to Shanghai on the morning of the 9th.

Ships Sheltering from Wind Set Sail One After Another

The China Merchants Bureau's Hairui Wheel, which loaded cargo from the Longhai Railway at Sunjiashan in Haizhou and set sail for Shanghai, encountered a typhoon as soon as it left the port. The ship did not dare to sail and immediately returned to Laoyao, and will set sail again today. The Beiyang regular Xinming Wheel encountered a typhoon on the way and entered Weihaiwei to take shelter. The Qihai Wheel, which was going to Fujian and was blocked in Wusong, had all set sail yesterday morning. The ships that were sheltering from the wind outside Wusongkou yesterday have entered the Pudong River one after another. Fortunately, precautions were taken in advance, so there were no accidents in this typhoon, which is also fortunate.

Shanghai-Ningbo Ferries Suspended Once

The Ningbo buses on the 7th were not issued, and the Ningxing, Xinjiangtian, and other buses that returned to Shanghai after leaving the port sailed as usual yesterday. Some of the passengers who had not refunded their tickets still took the original bus to Ningbo. The Xin Beijing and Ningshao buses from Ningbo are also expected to return to Shanghai this morning. During this strong wind, the Shanghai-Ningbo ferries of Sifen Company were suspended once.

Wang Kemin Went to Qing Yesterday

Departing on the Fengtian Maru

Wang Kemin, chief advisor to the North China Political Affairs Commission, has repeatedly delayed his trip due to connections with the banking community in Shanghai. Now that Huang Fu, who was staying in Moganshan, has gone down the mountain to Jiangxi, Wang Kemin departed from the Shanghai Bund at 9:00 AM yesterday on the Fengtian Maru for Qingdao to meet with Song Ziwen, lingered briefly, and returned directly to Beiping.

Hu Returns to Switzerland to Take Up His Post; Zhao Attends International Road Conference

Hu Shize, the Chinese ambassador to Switzerland, bid farewell to Wang as Foreign Minister in Beijing the day before yesterday and returned to Shanghai. Kong and His Wife Fly to Jiangxi This Morning

Stop Briefly in Beijing; Huang Fu May Travel with Them

According to the Central News Agency, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi has decided to fly to Jiangxi from Shanghai this morning around 9:00 AM, accompanied by his wife, Madame Song Ailing, and his daughter, Lingyi, on the Ford plane specially sent by Chairman Jiang to welcome Kong. After arriving in Jiangxi, in addition to attending a speech at the military officer training corps, Kong must also meet with President Wang, Chairman Jiang, and others to discuss political affairs. In other news, when Kong flies to Jiangxi via Beijing this morning on the Ford plane, he will stop briefly, because Huang Fu, the chairman of the Political Affairs Reorganization Committee stationed in Beijing, arrived in Beijing yesterday from Hangzhou and is scheduled to fly to Jiangxi on the same plane today.

Various Banks Submit to the Executive Yuan, etc.

Request to Amend the Savings Bank Law

Three Should Be Deleted, Two Should Be Amended

Rapid Enactment of Implementing Rules Can Provide Remedy

After the promulgation and implementation of the Savings Bank Law, the Banking Association invited all Chinese commercial banks in the city to hold a tea party to discuss and decide to request amendments. A reporter from New Voice obtained the Association's notice and submission from a certain bank last night, which are detailed below:

Association Notice

The Shanghai Banking Association notified various banks on the 8th of this month: We hereby inform you that on the 6th of this month, our Association invited all Chinese commercial banks in the city to hold a tea party to discuss the Savings Bank Law and the issue of requesting amendments. It was decided that the banks not in the Association should submit separate requests for amendments based on our Association's original draft submitted to the Ministry. The procedures for drafting and issuing them have been entrusted to our Association. We have printed and distributed the draft submission, along with the Savings Bank Law. Please review and study it. If you agree, please reply within two days so that we can draft it and send it to the banks for stamping and issuance as soon as possible. Please handle it urgently.

Presentation to the Ministry and Departments

Various banks petition the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, requesting amendments to the Savings Bank Law, stating that the Savings Bank Law should be carefully reviewed and amended to effectively protect depositors and facilitate its implementation. We believe that the essence of savings lies in accumulating small amounts to cultivate the habit of national savings and accumulate national capital. The division of bank deposits into fixed and current accounts is purely to meet the needs of depositors and their choices. The size of national savings reflects the overall economic strength of a country, and the ebb and flow of fixed and current deposits are inevitably subject to the magnitude of national savings. If various industries are developed, the national economy is prosperous, unemployment is not a concern, and life is stable, then savings will be greater, and depositors will naturally be happy to deposit into fixed-term deposits with higher interest rates. Conversely, if savings are very weak, any surplus funds are often prepared for temporary emergencies, and it is practically impossible to expect them to deposit more into fixed-term accounts. Therefore, depositors' choices of fixed or current accounts are entirely dictated by their savings capacity, and they themselves dare not act rashly. The government should not force them to choose, and banks have no way to accept or reject. According to Article 5 of this law, current deposits shall not exceed four-tenths of the total deposits. The legislative intent is to encourage the collection of more fixed deposits so that funds can be fully utilized, and market changes will not trigger a wave of withdrawals. The intention is profound, but banks and depositors will face great difficulties. As far as banks are concerned, the receipt and payment of deposits by banks vary from day to day, and it is impossible to match the proportions at all times. For those who have established branches in other cities, the total number cannot be calculated at that time, and there is no standard to follow. The bank is overwhelmed and exhausted to comply even for one day. As far as depositors are concerned, deposits were originally a matter of personal freedom. Now, with this regulation, depositors who deposit current accounts are likely to be rejected by the bank or have part of their deposits returned. Or even if they go to various banks, they may ultimately be unable to deposit due to the ratio limitation. Under such circumstances, it is enough to reduce the public interest in national savings and prevent the accumulation of national capital. The impact is significant. Depositors often deposit into current accounts first, and then convert to fixed accounts after accumulating a certain amount. In other words, current savings are the beginning of fixed savings. If restrictions are added, it is tantamount to cutting off the source. We should request that this restriction be deleted. Furthermore, national legislation should be long-lasting, so the meaning of the articles should be broad and not involve excessive details, and it should not be based on the special circumstances of one time and place as a standard. Article 8 of this law stipulates the composition restrictions on the use of funds. The legislative intent is to prevent the orientation of property and avoid crises, or to support rural areas to save the current evils. The legislative intent is recognized by everyone, but the trend of the times cannot be reversed. The prosperity and decline of economic undertakings and the supply and demand of investment matters also change with time. Especially since the amount of savings deposits received by various banks varies, it is difficult to adhere to one standard. Article 7 of this law has already limited its use, and all the paths of savings deposits within the scope of the restrictions do not need to be determined again to determine the investment policy based on time and place, so as to be flexible and profitable. Moreover, savings banks bear a greater responsibility than ordinary banks. For the sake of their own interests, practitioners will also do their best to ensure safety. After careful consideration, the provisions of Article 8 are not only too restrictive, but also may become ineffective after a long time. We should request that it be deleted. Furthermore, Article 7 of this law stipulates various items for the use of funds. The fourth item is to release funds pledged by fixed-term deposit certificates or passbooks of other banks. Although banks have the custom of accepting pledges of fixed-term deposit certificates of their own banks, it is not a prescribed business, so it can be handled flexibly. Now this law states that it can accept pledges of deposit certificates of other banks, then the scope is even wider. If there is a financial emergency, the law has already been stipulated, and there will inevitably be strong requests to accept pledges. It is extremely easy to cause misunderstandings and affect the market when banks are difficult to accept or reject. According to the banking habits of the United Kingdom and Japan, mortgages are also prohibited. This section is not very important and seems to be handled by banks in accordance with customs, which is more active. We should request that it be deleted. Furthermore, rural lending is a crucial plan in the entire national economy. However, for savings banks, in terms of ensuring the safety of depositors' funds, there are still points that should be noted. Most of the savings banks and commercial banks concurrently operating savings are now concentrated in cities. They are not familiar with rural lending, and they have more isolation from local conditions. Once they are forced to do it, there will be the worry of losing one thing or the other, or the worry of being unable to reach it. This is one. Our country's rural areas are disorganized, and the establishment of cooperatives in various places is not universal. Even in areas where cooperatives have been established, there are many cooperatives with substantial content, but also many with no substance and incomplete organizations. It is conceivable how dangerous it would be for savings banks that are not skilled in rural lending to engage in rural lending in a disorganized rural area. This is two. Agricultural funds focus on long-term low interest rates, but Article 8 of this law stipulates that loans pledged by rural cooperatives and loans pledged by agricultural products shall not be less than one-fifth of the total deposits. In other words, one-fifth of the deposits of savings banks have become fixed long-term loans. If the market changes, rural loans are not easy to recover, and the bank's fixed-term deposit certificates or passbooks cannot be refused for mortgage according to law. The impact is not only enough to shake the business of savings banks, but also loses the legislative purpose of protecting depositors. This is three. With these three points, the council will think again and again, and all agree that saving rural areas is an overall national policy. It should be planned by the state as a whole, and it should not be solely assigned to savings banks. The national rural economy and the conditions in various places are different. How should we consider the situation and take care of everything? Only the state can have this power. This power should be held by the state bank, and commercial banks and savings banks should follow suit. In this way, depositors' protection and rural relief will both benefit. This should be amended. Furthermore, savings banks are determined to be joint-stock limited companies, which is clearly stated in this law. Article 15 stipulates that directors and supervisors shall bear joint and several unlimited liability. It is assumed that the legislative authorities intend to stabilize depositors' protection and promote the self-respect of directors and supervisors. The intention is extremely profound. However, directors and supervisors are shareholders who perform business, and the greater the authority, the greater the responsibility. Before the enactment of this law, all banks automatically increased the responsibility of directors and supervisors, because there is a relationship between authority and responsibility. Now this law so restricts the savings business that it is strict and meticulous. Article 7 has listed the use of funds, and Article 8 stipulates the composition of its use. Directors and supervisors have no power to flexibly allocate. If they do not handle it in accordance with this law on weekdays, it is their fault if the bank suffers misfortune. Otherwise, if an accident occurs due to compliance with the law, they will still be liable for joint and several unlimited liability, which is not fair. The association admires the state's emphasis on savings and safeguarding the public interest, and has no intention of evading responsibility, but cannot bear the responsibility beyond compliance with the law. We should request that it be amended. Furthermore, domestic savings banks and banks that also handle savings have a considerable history. Foreign banks that also handle savings in China have never had restrictions. Each bank has its own special circumstances, which are extremely inconsistent. Once this law is implemented, there will be many problems. Moreover, are foreign banks that also handle savings subject to this law? If it cannot be universally applied, then domestic banks will not be able to develop due to excessive restrictions, or they will not be able to accept deposits as much as possible due to legal components. Chinese people's savings will inevitably be deposited in foreign banks, which is not the legislative policy. In addition, there are many clauses in this law that need to be explained and supplemented. In the era of metabolism and Sino-foreign mixes, implementing detailed rules should be formulated to remedy the situation and relax the implementation date to adjust. These points are all very important for long-term legislation. It is advisable to consider all aspects to eliminate obstacles and promote unhindered implementation. In this way, the savings business can be expected to grow, and depositors and banks will benefit from it. The association is concerned with its own interests, admires the government's purpose of promoting savings, and handles its own business seriously. It dares to express its opinions frankly and humbly requests the Ministry and departments to examine and approve it, and promptly re-examine and amend it, and wait for instructions. It is for the public good. Sincerely presented.

Page 13

Aftermath of the Rickshaw Dispute

Rickshaw Pullers Petitioned the Public Works Bureau Yesterday

Because the Newly Fixed Rental Fare Exceeded the Original Price

The Result of Petitioning the Vehicle Committee with Six Demands Was Satisfactory

A Few Rickshaw Pullers Caused Disturbances and Were Arrested and Released

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the rickshaw problem in the Public Concession has been resolved through mutual agreement. Rickshaw owners have begun to obtain licenses. Yesterday morning at 9 o'clock, more than 200 rickshaw pullers objected to the newly stipulated rental fare of 85 cents in silver dollars, which exceeded the original 11 cents in small dollars. They also objected to the rickshaw owners joining the mutual aid association and other matters. They specifically petitioned the Vehicle Committee of the Public Works Bureau, requesting the implementation of rickshaw puller registration and the early establishment of the mutual aid association, among other six demands. The details of the situation learned by the Xinxin News Agency reporter are recorded as follows:

Motivation for the Petition

The rickshaw pullers believe that the new method of resolving the issue through negotiation between the rickshaw owners and the Vehicle Committee has changed the original rental fare of 11 cents in small dollars to 85 cents in silver dollars. Based on the current prices, this is equivalent to 11 cents in small dollars plus 16 copper coins, which exceeds the original price and increases the burden on the rickshaw pullers. In addition, the rickshaw pullers' mutual aid association allows two representatives from the rickshaw owners to participate, which is inconsistent with the original purpose of the mutual aid association. At the same time, there are no clear provisions regarding the registration of rickshaw pullers and other issues, which has aroused resentment among the rickshaw pullers. Therefore, they specifically petitioned the Vehicle Committee, requesting a clear response.

Satisfactory Response

Yesterday morning at around 7 o'clock, more than 200 rickshaw pullers gathered in the Changsha Road and Xiaoshadu Road area to hold a temporary meeting. They resolved to make six demands for the purpose of the petition, and elected He Linsheng, Zhu Fengxiang, Cang Gongwen, Xu Xinglin, etc. to lead them directly to the Vehicle Committee of the Public Works Bureau to petition. Many rickshaw pullers from the Haotu rickshaw company also voluntarily joined. A member of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee met with them. The representatives made six requests, and the Vehicle Committee responded to each of them one by one. (1) Request that Mr. Massey, the chairman of the Vehicle Committee, not resign, and the rickshaw pullers unanimously retain him. (Answer) The rumor that Mr. Massey resigned is a misunderstanding. (2) Please continue to follow the original method, with a rental fare of 10 cents in small dollars per day, plus a mutual aid donation of 1 cent in small dollars. (Answer) Because the exchange rate between silver dollars and small dollars is unstable, the rental fare is stipulated in silver dollars. The current rental fare of 78 cents in silver dollars is equivalent to 10 cents in small dollars based on the average exchange rate in the first half of this year. (3) Oppose rickshaw owners joining the mutual aid association, because this association is funded by the rickshaw pullers themselves, and the rickshaw owners do not contribute any money. (Answer) Rickshaw owners do not join the mutual aid association's fund management committee. As for the two rickshaw owner representatives joining the association's board of directors, it is to express their intention to cooperate. In the future, they will be elected by the licensed rickshaw owners. Once the rickshaw puller registration is completed, the rickshaw pullers will elect two representatives to join the board of directors to jointly plan the process. (4) Mr. Cheng Xiechun is not a rickshaw puller and should not be a representative of the rickshaw pullers. (Answer) Mr. Cheng Xiechun's participation is based on his relationship as a fellow Jianghuai native, and he is not acting as a representative of the rickshaw pullers. (5) Rickshaw pullers should be registered immediately, four per rickshaw. (Answer) Rickshaw puller registration will begin soon and will still register four people per rickshaw according to the original plan. (6) Please have the Vehicle Committee preside over the establishment of a rickshaw pullers' mutual aid association as soon as possible. (Answer) The rickshaw pullers' mutual aid association will be established soon. The rickshaw pullers expressed satisfaction with the committee's responses and then dispersed.

Minor Disturbances

After the rickshaw pullers' appeal group petitioned the Public Works Bureau, a group of rickshaw pullers divided into teams, holding small flags and slogans, and ordered other rickshaw pullers to stop in various places such as Jiaxing Road, Kangdi Road, Disiwei Road, Kader Road, and Wuzhen Road Bridge, and deflated the rubber tires. Therefore, a large number of rickshaw pullers were unable to operate for a while, and the situation was quite chaotic. When the Rickshaw Owners Association received the news, they believed that this kind of action not only affected the business of the rickshaw owners but also concerned the livelihood of the rickshaw pullers. They immediately reported it to the Public Works Bureau. Chief Patrolman McTyeire ordered each police station to stop it and arrest them. More than 20 people were arrested by the Xinzha Road police station, more than 10 people by the Jiaxing Road police station, and a small number of people were arrested by other police stations. It was not until 4 pm that it was calm. It is reported that all those arrested have been released. The rickshaw owners sent people to various places to repair the vehicles and continue their business.

Remarks by the Vehicle Committee

Yesterday, the Xinxin News Agency reporter went to the Vehicle Committee to inquire about the new rickshaw owners. Committee member Wang Zhiren met with him and said that because the rickshaw owners had not come to obtain licenses in accordance with the new regulations previously issued by the committee, they had recruited new rickshaw owners to apply for registration. However, the committee had stated that when the vehicle licenses were exhausted, the guarantee money (5 yuan per vehicle) paid by the new rickshaw owners would be refunded in full. Now that the old rickshaw owners have complied with the amended new regulations and paid taxes and obtained licenses, there is no room to accommodate the newly registered rickshaw owners. Therefore, the committee issued a notice a few days ago. After the reporter finished speaking, he asked about the results of the rickshaw pullers' petition to the authorities this morning (that is, yesterday morning). Mr. Wang replied that the previous report that Mr. Massey, the chairman of the committee, had expressed negativity and would resign was absolutely incorrect. The rickshaw owners had voluntarily complied with the new regulations, and the only change was the rickshaw rental fare. However, there was little difference between the small dollar fluctuations and 85 cents in silver dollars. This point was purely a rumor. Because the general rickshaw pullers believed that Chairman Massey, who has always loved and protected the rickshaw pullers, would resign suddenly, the rickshaw pullers would feel more distressed. Therefore, they came to the committee to petition, requesting to cancel his resignation intention. Committee member Zhu Maocheng met with them and explained them one by one.

Statement by the Association

Yesterday, a person in charge of the Rickshaw Owners Association told a Xinxin News Agency reporter that at the meeting between the rickshaw owner representatives and the person in charge of the Public Works Bureau the day before yesterday, the rickshaw owners took into account the overall situation and avoided the escalation of the situation. They reluctantly accepted the various measures. The reduction of the rickshaw rental fare and the payment of mutual aid relief funds by the rickshaw owners all expressed the sincerity of the rickshaw owners in taking into account the overall situation and providing relief to the rickshaw pullers. The board of directors of the Public Works Bureau has already ratified it. Regrettably, this morning, so-called rickshaw puller representatives, such as Zheng Moumou, petitioned to oppose the resolutions of the Public Works Bureau and the rickshaw owner representatives, and shouted slogans supporting Massey. It is regrettable that these people claim to be representatives, but they are not rickshaw pullers themselves. It is difficult to understand where they obtained their representative status. The Rickshaw Affairs Management Committee summoned new rickshaw owners to register because it was afraid that the old rickshaw owners would refuse to obtain licenses. It also notified each registrant to comply with the regulations and pay the mutual aid fee and guarantee money. If they did not obtain a license, the guarantee money paid would be returned. This was purely a hypothetical preparation. Recently, it has been discovered that the number of vehicles specified in the notice is being sold at a price on the market to deceive the ignorant. Their speculation and cunning can be imagined. Now that the Public Works Bureau's announcement states that the old rickshaw owners are complying with the regulations and obtaining licenses, the registration of new rickshaw owners will be invalid. Therefore, speculation has failed, and they are posing as rickshaw pullers to engage in disturbances. The rickshaws and rickshaw pullers who were forced to accompany them along the way are still unaware of the truth and meaning under their threats. In several places, it was discovered that rubber tires were being violently deflated and rickshaw pullers were prohibited from operating. Endangering business and disrupting public order is extremely illegal. If this continues, it will affect social stability. The association, in addition to separately submitting requests to the police authorities for a serious investigation and thorough investigation in accordance with the law, has been informed that Chief Patrolman McTyeire has ordered each police station to arrest the ringleaders and detain them for strict punishment. He has also notified each rickshaw owner to inform the rickshaw pullers in the city of the truth of this incident so that they will not be used by them.

City Federation

Sent Three Important Letters to the Public Works Bureau Yesterday

Request to Improve Educational Administration in the Public Concession

Do Not Overestimate Property Donations or Increase Hotel Industry Donations

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation, in order to request the Public Works Bureau to improve educational administration in the Public Concession and cancel the overestimation of property donations and the increase in hotel industry donation amounts, specifically sent letters to the administrative authorities of the Public Works Bureau yesterday. The original letters are recorded separately as follows:

Letter 1

Dear Sir,

The educational expenses in the concession are wasted to hundreds of thousands every year. The Chinese citizens fulfill the obligation of paying taxes, but the right to enjoy education is very small. Considering the reasons, although the Public Concession Public Works Bureau's school management office is established, it does not actually examine the educational situation. It should be reformed or schools should be opened. It follows unbreakable rules. For example, school health inspectors hire Westerners, using Westerners who do not understand the situation of Chinese schools and have no research on school health to fill the post. It is really inappropriate. As for management, it also lacks the experience of managing Chinese education. Therefore, to improve education in the concession, it must be supervised by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau in administration, and a special committee should be formed to be responsible for designing to improve the educational facilities in the concession. We hope that your bureau will take measures as soon as possible and proceed accordingly. It would be the education's fortune and the citizens' fortune.

Letter 2

Dear Sir,

We have received a letter from the 10th district branch of this association stating that Jin Chang Factory, a member at No. 499 Zhoujiazui Road, claims that the factory building has been built for many years and its rent is estimated by the Public Works Bureau to be 50 yuan per month. The municipal general donation is calculated according to 50 yuan (that is, 7 yuan per month). Unexpectedly, the Public Works Bureau suddenly accounted for as high as 150 yuan per month, which is twice as much as the original amount, which is really unbearable. It requires negotiations and still pays donations according to the original amount. Based on this, it has been investigated and confirmed that this is the truth. This random valuation is really wrong. It is important to know that the exercise of municipal powers should first be unified. If you play around arbitrarily, turn right and wrong upside down, it will disrupt the municipal administration more than this. We should write to your bureau to investigate and correct it according to reason, and do not overestimate it arbitrarily to maintain the municipal administration. We sincerely hope.

Letter 3

Dear Sir,

We have received a letter from the Shanghai Hotel Industry Association stating that according to reports from members such as Dongfang Dachunghua, the Public Works Bureau sent personnel to investigate room prices and re-accounted for the total value of the house. Starting in October, it will increase to one-third and one-half. In this time of market depression, how can we bear it? Our association, for the survival of the hotel industry, and for the prevention of other industries, will definitely adhere to it consistently. We sincerely ask your association to uphold justice, help with all your strength, and transfer to the Public Works Bureau to negotiate, withdraw its order, and maintain the dying hotel industry. We are looking forward to it. After the sixth executive committee meeting, it was decided to write to the Public Works Bureau to maintain business difficulties and withdraw the agreed-upon opinion. We should write to ask for your consideration.

Wheat and Cotton Gradually Transported to Shanghai

American wheat loans, according to the contract, were to be fully loaded in the United States by the end of June and arrive in Shanghai by the end of August. However, due to the strike, ships carrying wheat were stranded in Portland and could not depart, causing the wheat ordered by various factories in Shanghai to be delayed. Now that the strike has ended, American wheat is being loaded in large quantities for Shanghai. Yesterday, this port received a telegram stating that 9,700 tons could arrive in Shanghai on the 12th of this month. Workers are being prepared for unloading. Three more ships, carrying over 20,000 tons, have also set sail from the United States and are expected to arrive and be delivered in Shanghai by the end of this month at the latest, with all shipments completed within ten days.

In addition to wheat, there is still a large amount of flour, totaling over 200,000 tons, included in the American loan. Initially, the shipment was delayed because there was no way to sell this flour in Shanghai. However, now that North China is in urgent need of wheat flour and factories in Shanghai are unable to keep up with production, the batch of over 200,000 tons of loan flour has also begun to be loaded onto ships in the United States and is expected to arrive in large quantities early next month. It is said that the Economic Commission will allocate a portion to be transferred to the Northwest for the purpose of subsidizing the development of the Northwest.

Two batches of American cotton, totaling over 39,000 bales, have already arrived and been fully unloaded at the Chinese warehouses. The third batch has already been loaded and is en route. It was originally scheduled to arrive on the 15th, but due to slight delays en route for the "Adigan Sea" (carrying 15,500 bales) and the "Aysania United" (carrying 1,740 bales), the arrival date has been changed to the 22nd of this month. There are also two more ocean liners, the fifth and sixth batches, carrying a total of over 19,000 pieces of cotton. According to a telegram yesterday, they are expected to arrive in Shanghai around September 15th and will be unloaded at the Chinese warehouses. In addition, 19,500 bales of cotton directly purchased by Japanese merchants in Shanghai from the United States are also expected to arrive on the 15th of this month.

Inconsistencies are especially evident everywhere in our country's government orders. Even with the sanctity of the judiciary, simple lawsuit matters cannot be standardized. Moreover, the cost of lawsuit paper is estimated to be only about four or five cents. The court is not a profit-making enterprise and should not sell lawsuit paper that costs four or five cents for ninety cents or sixty cents in one place, and forty-five cents or thirty cents in another. Even if judicial funding is insufficient, the government should find ways to allocate funds. If it is absolutely necessary to collect from the people, it should be clearly stipulated in laws and regulations and formally collected. It does not seem appropriate to use pretenses to raise the price of lawsuit paper, which is an act close to the monopoly of goods and arbitrary price increases, leaving a stain on the judicial organs. This is the first matter that should be corrected. Furthermore, the Shanghai courts, the First Special District Local Court, have only recently started calculating interest on the funds deposited by the parties involved (but the use of the interest collected in the past has not been disclosed). Other courts, such as the Second Special District Local Court and the Local Court, have not yet calculated interest on the funds deposited by the parties involved. This is not only the case in Shanghai but is likely true for judicial courts across the country. Ancient sages said, "Rectify oneself and then rectify things." The court's responsibility is to protect the rights of the people based on the law. Rectifying oneself and rectifying things is what it should do. The court itself should not have or obtain undue benefits. This is the second matter that should be corrected. The above two cases are matters that the court itself should correct. We, who cherish the judiciary, have dared not remain silent as far as our limited knowledge extends. We plan to ask the assembly to discuss and suggest that the Judicial Administration Department issue a notice to the whole country to find ways to correct these matters in order to maintain judicial authority. Based on this, the 174th joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees of the association resolved to make recommendations to the Ministry for adoption and implementation. It is appropriate to submit a document to the Ministry for review and implementation, which would be of public benefit. Respectfully submitted to the Judicial Administration Department by the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Lawyers Association.

The Jianghai Customs Responds to the Ministry of Finance

Strict Prohibition of Private Transportation of Copper Coins and Inferior Small Coins

The Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office yesterday responded to the Ministry of Finance, stating (omitted above): The customs office has always been extremely strict in inspecting the private transportation of silver coins and copper coins. We have repeatedly received your orders, which have been forwarded to customs officials to handle with diligence. Now that we have received orders to strictly investigate and prohibit, we have forwarded them to the Tax Affairs Department for compliance. According to their response, the customs office has followed the government's clear orders and established measures to strictly investigate and prevent this matter. The recent decrease in the number of smuggling cases detected does not mean that the prohibition order has not been strictly enforced, but rather that the customs' strict prevention has deterred smugglers from passing through the customs' jurisdiction. However, since the previous instructions have been forwarded, in addition to reiterating to customs officials that any copper coins and inferior silver coins transported without permission should be detained, we also request your review, etc. All reasons for the customs office's crackdown on the private transportation of copper coins and silver coins have been forwarded to the customs for compliance. The Beijing-Shanghai Highway

The Entire New Long-Distance Telephone Line is Completed

Currently Continuing to Lay Local Lines in Various Districts

Direct Dialing Throughout the Line is Not Far Off

The Beijing-Shanghai long-distance telephone line was originally set up along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, with a total of three pairs of lines. However, due to the heavy traffic during peacetime, it was insufficient for use. In order to facilitate the flow of information between Beijing and Shanghai, the Ministry of Communications specially allocated funds to lay several pairs of long-distance telephone lines along the Beijing-Shanghai Highway. Since the commencement of construction this spring, most of the project has been completed. The route passes through Nanjing, Liyang, Yixing, Wuxi, Changshu, Taicang, Jiading, and reaches Shanghai. According to the Long-Distance Telephone Office, as of the middle of last month, three pairs of long-distance telephone lines on this highway have been installed. The remaining three pairs of lines were also fully installed last Sunday. Currently, telephone sets are being installed and the installation of local lines connecting Changshu, Wuxi, and other places is continuing in order to enable communication between districts first and then determine the date for direct dialing throughout the line. In the future, telephone communication between Beijing and Shanghai will no longer be subject to interruptions and congestion, and will be much more convenient than before.

The Municipal Government Convenes Various Groups

To Discuss Methods for Dredging the Wusong River

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the dredging of the Wusong River is related to the water conservancy of Shanghai, Baoshan, Suzhou, Songjiang, Jiading, Daguan, and Qingpu counties, providing irrigation for over 8 million acres of farmland. Unfortunately, due to prolonged neglect, the river channel has become increasingly silted up. Local gentry have attempted to find ways to dredge it, but ultimately gave up due to lack of funds. Now, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has decided on a dredging plan. The Municipal Government believes that the Wusong River is related to a significant amount of farmland and intends to resolve the issue as soon as possible in order to proceed simultaneously. We have learned that Mayor Wu is scheduled to convene representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Shipping Association, and the directors of the Finance, Public Works, and Engineering Bureaus, as well as relevant personnel from the Municipal Government, at the Municipal Government at 10:00 am today to discuss dredging methods in order to start construction.

Page 14

The Public Works Bureau's Transportation Committee

Discusses Pedestrian Safety Measures

Most Injured Pedestrians are Illiterate

Nine out of Ten are Crossing Roads

During a recent meeting, the Public Works Bureau's Transportation Committee thoroughly discussed two methods proposed by a director to increase the protection of pedestrians on the streets within the concession: (1) The dangers of crossing or lingering on the streets should be widely publicized in important locations. (2) A safe zone should be designated for pedestrians crossing the streets, similar to other well-known cities. According to the police chief's report, most pedestrians injured in accidents on the streets are illiterate, so the usefulness of danger notices is questionable. Pedestrian accidents often occur at street intersections because they attempt to cross the road quickly in front of fast-moving vehicles. The current method is for lecturers to give speeches to the public on the method of "seeking safety first when walking." Most major road intersections have pedestrian lanes marked with yellow paint, but few people use them. As for building safety islands, the streets within the concession are generally narrow, and major thoroughfares such as Nanjing Road and Jing'an Temple Road have tram tracks, leaving no room for the installation of such islands. Later, a committee member inquired with the police chief, who replied that accidents involving pedestrians on the streets occur in locations where crossing the road is not allowed, accounting for approximately nine out of ten cases. Another committee member said that since there is no detailed investigation into all the important causes of pedestrian accidents on the streets, the police chief's report is the only answer to the suggestions made in this case. The city of Bodu in the United States once tried to order pedestrians to cross the street only at designated locations or to follow the instructions of traffic controllers, but it was ineffective because the public did not cooperate with this method. The traffic problem in Shanghai is one of the most difficult in the world. Partial measures cannot be adopted without thoroughly studying the entire problem of traffic management from all aspects. All accidents on the streets of American cities have detailed records of classification and listing in order to determine the causes of the accidents. It is believed that the police departments of American cities will be happy to share the methods used to classify and analyze accidents on the streets, and the news about these methods will be of great benefit to the study of traffic management problems in this port. After discussion, the committee believed that the police chief's report was a sufficient answer to the methods proposed by a director. However, the problem of pedestrian traffic is becoming increasingly important and should continue to be noted by the police chief at all times.

X X X X

During the Typhoon the Other Day

Many Boats Capsized at the Mouth of the Wusong River

Four Pig Boats Sunk

The Jiangbei pig boat Ni Changtai loaded 160 live pigs from the Ni Shengji pig business in Xinsheng Port on the 7th of this month, intending to sell them in Shanghai. At 11:00 am on the 8th, when it sailed to the coast opposite the Lion Forest outside the Wusong River mouth, it encountered a typhoon. It was unable to withstand the direct hit and was capsized by huge waves. The live pigs were also lost with the boat. Six crew members and six pig merchants (a total of twelve people) fell into the water with the boat. Fortunately, the Chongming ship Jingde passed by and immediately threw two lifebuoys, rescuing crew member Chen Wenfu and pig merchant Yao Dareen, who were able to survive. They were sent ashore in Wusong on that ship. The two immediately reported the details of the accident to the Shanghai Municipal Pig Industry Wusong Delivery Office and requested rescue. Director Hong Wenjiang of the office inquired about the situation and first sent the injured pig merchant Yao Dareen to Yuanshun Pig Business for treatment at the hospital. He then tried to find the whereabouts of the ten missing crew members, including the helmsman Liu Lujin. Until yesterday morning, six crew members and pig merchants, including Liu Lujin, arrived in Wusong and claimed that they had been hit by a typhoon and washed up on the beach by huge waves. They were rescued by the British merchant ship Ruihe of Jardine Matheson and taken to the ship. Loan Dispute with the Bank of Communications

Fu Xiaoan Sues Lawyer Yan Dajue

Lawyer Yan Sends a Letter to Fu on Behalf of Dai Zhenwu

Fu Believes it Has Intimidating Intent and Sues in Court

丨Lawyer Yan also Files a Counterclaim Against Fu丨

Fu Xiaoan, a well-known figure from Ningbo, served as the manager of the Bank of Communications in the 16th year of the Republic of China. Later, due to political reasons, he was wanted by the National Government. Therefore, his vacant position as manager of the Bank of Communications was succeeded by Wang Xinguan. Wang's relative, Dai Zhenwu, also known as Shengzu, the owner of the Japanese-owned Dai Shengchang Shipping Company, borrowed over 110,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications on behalf of Fu. Dai signed a promissory note and gave it to Wang for safekeeping. Last year, after Wang Xinguan died of illness, Fu was also able to cancel the wanted order, so he returned to his original position. Fu then proposed this promissory note at a board meeting of the bank, wanting to sue Dai for the previous loan. Although the directors

Did Not Approve

Fu insisted strongly and sued the Japanese consulate, claiming that Dai was a Japanese merchant. Dai then hired the Japanese lawyer Yano Nobuo to negotiate the lawsuit with Fu, but because Yano had not registered with the Chinese court, he commissioned the Cantonese lawyer Yan Dajue as his sub-agent, sending a letter to Fu Xiaoan outlining the process and setting a deadline for a response, otherwise he would file a lawsuit. The letter was sent on June 25th. After Fu received the letter, he believed that Lawyer Yan should not collude to intimidate him and immediately commissioned Lawyer Dai Chengxiang to send a letter to Yan. Yan then instructed Dai Zhenwu to produce

Relevant Evidence

Dai immediately handed over a photo of a letter from Wang Xinguan, stating that the staff of the Bank of Communications and the Ningbo people in Shanghai all knew about the matter of raising funds on behalf of Fu. Fu then extended Lawyer Dai to file a lawsuit with the criminal court of the First Special Court, accusing Yan Dajue of intimidation. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 pm, Judge Liu Yugui held a hearing in the eighth criminal court. Yan extended Lawyer Sheng Peidong to turn himself in and presented a defense and a counterclaim in court. Plaintiff Fu Xiaoan did not arrive and Lawyer Dai stated the main points of the prosecution, saying that the "board of directors Fu strongly advocated suing for the loan" in Yan's letter, and "compensating for the damage to reputation and money, limited to a clear response within five days, otherwise a private prosecution" were

Intimidating Intent

requesting that it be handled according to law. Defendant Yan Dajue also detailed the process, saying that Dai Zhenwu originally entrusted the case of suing Fu Xiaoan to the Japanese lawyer Yano Nobuo in Shanghai. Yano had not been registered and could not appear in the Chinese court, so he transferred the case to the defense lawyer as a sub-agent. After accepting this sub-agency case, the defense lawyer gradually inquired about the facts and intended to file a lawsuit on his behalf. However, he heard that Fu Xiaoan was a person of considerable status, so he first sent a letter based on the facts, asking him to respond clearly within a time limit, in order to clarify the right and wrong of the two parties, or perhaps someone could mediate and settle the dispute. After the draft of the letter was prepared, it was still given to Yano to read and obtain his consent, believing that it was not contrary to the meaning of the entrusted matter. After his

Approval and Stamping

it was returned to the defense lawyer, who then made a copy and sent it out. Later, he met directly with Dai Zhenwu and conducted an investigation based on the facts stated by Yano. The so-called "a letter from the three gentlemen to me," Dai Zhenwu showed a photo of the letter, and the defense lawyer believed it to be true and handed over the photo to be attached to the dossier as evidence of the facts of the prosecution. After the letter was sent by the defense lawyer, he received a reply from Lawyer Dai Chengxiang on behalf of Fu Xiaoan within a few days, saying that it was a fabrication of intimidation and that Lawyer Yan was an accomplice and would be dealt with separately, etc. The defense lawyer then went to inquire about Yano with the letter, and Yano also presented a duplicate of his preparation document submitted to the Shanghai Japanese Consulate

Civil Defense

to prove that it was indeed the case and not a fabrication. At that time, Dai Zhenwu said that there was talk of an out-of-court settlement and instructed the defense lawyer to postpone the lawsuit, so the indictment paper that had already been signed is still shelved at the defense lawyer's office. Judging from this period of accepting the case, it is sufficient to prove that the defense lawyer handled it with caution, and it can be known that there was absolutely no fabrication of facts by the party involved. How can the plaintiff falsely accuse the defense lawyer of being an accomplice in intimidation? Based on the above defense, the defense lawyer absolutely had no suspicion of fabricating facts and colluding in intimidation with the party involved Dai Zhenwu, but the plaintiff actually resented and implicated the defense lawyer for acting as an agent in the lawsuit, falsely accusing him of being

An Accomplice in Intimidation

and filing a private prosecution with your court, intending to have the defense lawyer subjected to criminal punishment. He should be requested to be punished for the crime of false accusation in accordance with Article 180, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and to attach a civil lawsuit requesting a judgment ordering compensation for damage to reputation. Based on the above statements, it should be announced that the defense lawyer is innocent and that the defendant in the counterclaim is guilty of false accusation, and that he should be ordered to compensate for damage to reputation. Judge Liu verified the confession, and since the defendant in this case had already filed a counterclaim, the defendant in the counterclaim should also be brought to court in accordance with the law. He then instructed that the case be rescheduled for August 17th in the afternoon and that the plaintiff Fu Xiaoan be brought to court for questioning. The court was adjourned and it was already dusk.

Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau

Strictly Prohibits Adulteration of Tea Leaves

Adulteration of tea leaves is strictly prohibited. According to a recent report from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, Pingyang, Zhejiang is a famous tea-producing area. The Tea Industry Association of the county has conducted serious inspections to eliminate fake tea. Unscrupulous merchants know that they cannot succeed and have designed roundabout routes to transport exports from Shacheng, Ruian, and other places. If strict inspections are not carried out, the impact on the tea products of the association will be significant. After receiving the report, the Commodity Inspection Bureau, in addition to paying special attention to inspections, also sent a letter to the Ruian County Government requesting that it issue a strict prohibition on the bad habit of adulteration.

Fake Business Name

Defrauds Out-of-Town Customers

Victims from Various Places Report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau

Investigation Reveals that the Trademark Number Belongs to Lei Yushang

The house at No. 73 Tongchang Lane, Haining Road, Public Concession, Shanghai, is rented by Li Xingchun, a Cantonese chef at the Xinghualou Restaurant on Simalu Road. On February 10th of this year, two men with accents from Jiading and Nanxiang suddenly appeared, claiming to be Zhang and Zhao, requesting to sublet the house. Li happened to be out, and Li's wife received them. She saw that the two men behaved generously and were neatly dressed, quite like upper-class people, so she did not doubt them and agreed to sublet the house, saying that it was for the purpose of opening a business name as a wholesale point, with a factory in Nanyang. After the rent was paid, no lease contract was signed. They moved in immediately, set up their business, and placed advertisements in various newspapers, falsely claiming that they had registered with the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry in 1928 and obtained a license number 103, and a certificate number 37 issued by the Capital National Goods Exhibition Hall for participating in the Jiangsu Specialty Exhibition, in order to celebrate their 12th anniversary, promote domestic cotton textiles, and send out sample notices. At the same time, they distributed 500 gift vouchers in various provinces and cities across the country, stating that for every 8.50 yuan sent abroad, they would send 62 kinds of sample goods, along with a price list of the above domestic goods samples. They also claimed that after receiving the payment, they would send a shipping notice in two boxes by the post office customs broker, using red-cornered printed stationery and envelopes. The price list was also very gorgeous. As a result, many people from provinces, cities, counties, towns, and villages sent letters to purchase the goods. It is said that the amount of money obtained by fraud was very large, which is quite shocking. Until April 10th, the two men, who claimed to be Zhang and Zhao, disappeared without a trace and sealed the back door key in a letter, leaving it on the window of the house for the second landlord to open, falsely claiming that they had been ordered to close down and had already wound up, and that all the belongings existed to pay the rent. It was stated that there were no names. After Li Xingchun opened and disassembled it, he realized that he had been deceived. Later, after the payment was made, letters came from various places urging them to send the 62 kinds of sample goods, but they had already fled without a trace. It is said that those who were defrauded included the county magistrate of Qian'an, Hebei, the Nanggong County Government, the Laibin County Government, Li Zongwu of the Third Section, the Anyou County Public Security Bureau, the Jishan County Public Security Bureau of Shanxi Province, and the director of the Xinbi County Public Security Bureau of Hubei Province, and so on. They have sent written complaints to the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, accusing the factory of setting up a scam to obtain money, and the cases are piling up like mountains, along with the deceptive statements sent by the factory, falsely claiming that "Our factory recently suffered a fire in the neighborhood, which caused a lot of damage to the machines and goods. If you can't wait, please let us know and we can return the money." The printing and letters are quite amusing. After Director Wen received this large number of written complaints, in addition to submitting a request to the Municipal Government to investigate whether the factory had registered with the Ministry of Industry, he also ordered Hong Qi, the chief of the Second Section of the Bureau, to send Wang Guoxian, the director of the Commercial Affairs Division, to investigate the results. According to reporters, the Municipal Government has investigated with the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and other departments that the license number 103 and the certificate number 37 issued by the Capital National Goods Exhibition Hall for the Jiangsu Specialty Exhibition are the licenses of the Lei Yushang Songfen Tang Medicinal Materials Company. Therefore, after Director Wen received the order, he has issued a wanted order to his subordinates to arrest the fleeing scammers and bring them to justice.

Death by Stealing Watermelons

Qu Atao Dies Tragically

Qu Atao, a 30-year-old man from Huangdu, used to be a fruit vendor, but recently became unemployed. This summer, he partnered with a friend to transport watermelons for sale. This time, he hired Wang Jiangyin's lighter to load more than 100 dan of watermelons from the Fangtai area of Huangdu. Qu Atao was in charge of the boat. At about 2:00 pm the day before yesterday, it sailed to the west end of the Xinqiao bridge at the Sampan Factory. There were more than a dozen ruffians from other places who were swimming in the river. When they saw Qu's watermelon boat, they rushed forward to block it and demand watermelons. Qu saw that there were many of them and did not dare to refuse, so he had to reluctantly give them four watermelons. Unexpectedly, they claimed that they had to have twenty. Qu refused to agree, and the ruffians became angry. They dragged Qu Atao into the river and forcibly dragged Wang Jiangyin. Wang saw that the situation was bad and grabbed the side of the boat. Fortunately, he did not fall into the water, but after Qu Atao was dragged into the water, he drowned because he did not know how to swim. Later, the ruffians saw that they had caused a great disaster and fled in all directions. Wang Jiangyin was shocked and cried for help. With the help of others, he took Qu Atao's body to report to the Water Patrol Squad to arrest the fleeing criminals and notified Qu Ajin, the father of the deceased in Huangdu, and Qu Wang, the wife of the deceased, who came to Shanghai overnight to mourn the body. Yesterday morning, Lu Abao, the local security guard of the 11th district, reported to the local court. Prosecutor Lei Binzhang, along with examiner Xuan Zhiming, went to investigate.

Legal Case Regarding Hemorrhoid Removal

Hemorrhoid Tube Inside Glass Bottle

It Was Merely a Doctor's Deliberate Mystification

Ge Heqing Was Fooled, He Rongzhou Is Despicable

Ge Heqing, a clerk from the Zhongfu Bank on Hong Kong Road and a native of Ningbo, is 42 years old and resides at No. 2 Zhenru Lane, Kaizier Road in the French Concession. Ge had been suffering from hemorrhoids for a while and had been unable to find a good doctor to treat them. On the 12th of last month, introduced by a friend Xin Youjin, he sought treatment from He Rongzhou, a Jiangbei quack doctor residing at No. 58 Taihe Lane, Buer Road. At that time, both parties agreed on a medical fee of 42 silver dollars, with 6 dollars paid upfront and the remaining balance to be paid upon successful treatment. They also agreed to perform surgery on the 14th. When the date arrived, Ge went to He's place as agreed. He pretended to perform surgery, instructing Ge to lie on the bed and then performed an incision, cutting off the tube of the external hemorrhoid from the anus. He then placed this tube in a small glass medicine bottle and showed it to Ge, claiming that this was the root of the disease and that now that it had been removed, his suffering would be eliminated from then on, and he would recover in a few days. Ge was overjoyed and believed it to be true, thinking that after the hemorrhoid tube was removed, he would no longer suffer. However, he then became suspicious as to why he felt no pain despite having undergone surgery. Nevertheless, he paid the remaining 36 dollars of the medical fee in full. He took the hemorrhoid tube in the bottle home. Unexpectedly, after several days, Ge's hemorrhoids relapsed, and he still felt unbearable pain in his anus. He then realized that the root of the disease had not been removed. Therefore, he sent the hemorrhoid tube cut off by Dr. He to the famous doctor Zhang Xinghai for examination. After examination, Dr. Zhang found that the item in the bottle was not an external hemorrhoid tube but resembled a grass root. At this point, Ge realized he had been deceived and reported it to the French police, requesting an investigation. The police chief approved and dispatched detective Gong Wenlang to arrest He Rongzhou and bring him to the police station. The police chief asked him if he had a doctor's diploma or a license from the French Municipal Council. He replied that he did not. The police chief said that since He had neither a doctor's certificate nor a Municipal Council license, he was clearly a quack doctor endangering the public, which was no small matter, and was guilty of fraud under Article 363 of the criminal law, as well as violating Ordinance No. 205 for doctors practicing medicine issued by the French Consulate and Ordinance No. 115 for shops issued by the French Consul. He was ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, where Judge Wu Fanglian interrogated him. Police lawyer Yao Zhaodi explained the case, followed by a statement from the plaintiff Ge Heqing, who stated that he was currently being mediated by friends and requested the case to be withdrawn. The judge instructed that this case was not one that could be withdrawn at will. Ge then gave a detailed account of how he sought medical treatment and was deceived. When asked, He Rongzhou confessed that when the plaintiff came to him for treatment, a lot of pus and blood flowed from his anus, which healed after he performed surgery and applied medicine. As for the contents of the bottle, it was actually a pus and blood tube from the anus. Now that the plaintiff did not want to pay, he could return the money in full, etc. Judge Wu reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to pay a deposit of 300 yuan to be released on bail, pending a further hearing on the 13th. He also ordered the contents of the bottle to be sent to the forensic doctor for examination to determine whether it was actually a tube or something else.

Bi Furui Embezzlement Case

Both Sides Hope for Reconciliation

Adjourned for Another Week

Bi Furui, the accounting director of the Beipiao Coal Mining Company's Shanghai warehouse, was arrested for stealing the property of his aunt Xu Bi (i.e., Xu Wutaitai of Shengze) worth over 100,000 yuan stored in the vault of the Zhongnan Bank. The case was investigated by the police, who arrested Bi and his father, brother, and Wang Fusheng, and transferred them to the First Special District Court. Because there was hope for reconciliation, everyone except Bi Furui was released on bail. This has been reported in this newspaper several times. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhan Liangce continued the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. The defendant's lawyers Fan Gang and Yuan Yang'an stated the status of the reconciliation, saying that after the adjournment, with the mediation of relatives and friends from both sides, Bi Furui had gradually repaid the money with his salary, and the Bi family's land was offset against the plaintiff's losses. The only unresolved issue was that the plaintiff needed to pay a sum of cash upfront. It was initially agreed to pay 5,000 yuan upfront, but Bi Furui needed to go out and arrange for the funds, so they requested the court to allow Bi Furui to be released on bail. However, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that he did not know the details of the reconciliation. According to the plaintiff's statement to his lawyer, he only wanted the case to be concluded as soon as possible, so he requested that the trial proceed. Judge Zhan then ruled to proceed with the trial. As the police lawyer Qian Xunjiu was about to explain the case, lawyers Fan and Yuan immediately said that the reconciliation of the case was already in sight, and requested the court to consider that both sides were relatives. Once the trial began, it would inevitably fail. They requested the court to revoke the ruling to help them complete the reconciliation. Judge Zhan approved, revoked the judgment, and adjourned the case for one week. Bi Furui was allowed to be released on bail with a deposit of 5,000 yuan.

French Concession Municipal Federation

Continued Hearing on Opposition to Water and Electricity Price Increases

Municipal Federation Fourth Branch Sends Letter to Taxpayers' Association

Fifth Branch Schedules Meeting to Discuss

According to the Guowen News Agency, the French commercial water and electricity company in the French Concession of this port recently changed the regulations for the supply of water and electricity, increasing the old security deposit (i.e., cabinet deposit) and meter installation fees several times. Starting from July of this year, all users should wait for the new agreement to be implemented. After receiving the notice from the company, all stores in the French Concession were panicked, feeling that in this economic downturn, they could not afford this disguised price increase with huge deposits. They unanimously expressed their opposition and jointly sent a letter to the Municipal Federation, advocating fairness and negotiating on the basis of reason. The Fourth Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Municipal Federation sent a separate letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession and the Second Municipal Federation, requesting negotiations on the basis of reason. The Fifth Branch also announced the convening of a meeting to discuss countermeasures. The original letters and announcements of the two associations are transcribed below.

Letter to Taxpayers' Association

To Whom It May Concern,

We have learned that the French commercial water and electricity company recently secretly requested the French Municipal Council to change the regulations, increase the meter installation fee, and the huge cabinet deposit. At a time when the market is depressed, all industries are declining, and the livelihoods of the citizens are in danger, the French Municipal Council did not consider it and was secretly requested. According to the council's bulletin, the company's request stated that it was giving up the price increase request made in 1932 and instead implemented a huge increase in the cabinet deposit. This action is no different from a disguised price increase. Water and electricity are public utilities, and their main purpose is to facilitate the citizens, unlike other profit-making businesses. Moreover, the company earns more than one million yuan a year and is still not satisfied, being greedy and insatiable, only seeking profit, disregarding the current situation of commercial fatigue, and the economic distress of the citizens. Arbitrarily disguised price increases are unreasonable. Our association has received repeated requests from citizens in the district to oppose and prevent this disguised price increase in order to alleviate the burden. After convening an emergency meeting for discussion, it was unanimously agreed that under the current economic downturn, with general overproduction and falling prices, public utilities should reduce their prices to save the situation. Now, the purpose is to increase prices, which the citizens cannot afford. It was unanimously decided to write to your association, requesting you to forward the letters to the Chinese directors, and suggest to the French Municipal Council to quickly stop the company from changing the regulations to avoid disguised price increases and secure the citizens and alleviate their burden. Therefore, we are sending this letter to your association for your prompt handling.

Fifth Branch Announcement

To Whom It May Concern,

Our association has received statements from members such as the Zhonghua Factory on Caishi Road, stating that they have received a notice from the French commercial water and electricity company that the water and electricity deposit will be increased from July. We were shocked to read it. Merchants are having difficulty maintaining their businesses in this time of economic recession, how can they afford this huge cabinet deposit? They request reasonable negotiations and strong opposition. Our association has scheduled an emergency meeting to be held at the association office at the intersection of Laoshifu Road at 3:00 pm on the 12th of this month to discuss countermeasures. We hope you will attend on time and not delay.
